 Turmeric used as a spice in Indian homes is very beneficial for health
 haldi khaane kaa swaad badhaane ke saath sadiyon se kai sehat sambandhit kai samasyaon ke ilaaj ke liye istemaal kii ja rahi he
 It has been confirmed in many studies that the intake of turmeric benefits both body and mind
 haldi jodon or gathiya ke dard main bhi bahut phydemand hoti he
 These are the benefits of turmeric - Improve the digestive system - If you are suffering from stomach problems, then turmeric intake will benefit
 ayurveda main sadiyon se haldi kaa istemaal digeshan ko behatar karne ke liye kiya ja rahaa he
 Turmeric has anti-oxidant and anti-inflammatory properties, which helps the digestive system improve 
 study ke mutabik, haldi ke seven gas kii samasya bhi dur hoti he
 Healthy Skin - Turmeric is very effective in removing wrinkles on the face from growing age
 haldi main anti-oxidative or anti-inflametry gun paae jate hai
 They help in removing facial wrinkles
 rojaanaa haldi kaa seven karne se skin par glo aata he
 Strengthens immunity - Turmeric is also found to have a Lipopolysaccharide compound with anti-bacterial, anti-viral and anti-fungal properties
 haldi ke seven se immunity power majboot hoti he or aap kai tarah ke infections se surakshit rahete hai
 Taking one spoon of turmeric with a glass of warm milk daily can help in getting relief from cold, cold, flu etc
 dimag ke liye phydemand-haldi main maujuud Aromatic Turmerone compound dimag ke liye bahut phydemand hota he
 This causes the repair of brain stem cells
 iske alaava haldi main maujuud karcumin bhi dimag main paae jane vaale protein ko boost karata he
 Helpful in losing weight - Nowadays most people are upset with their increasing weight

 jaaniye kaise aap ghar baithe itiar (ITR) yani inakam tex ritern file kar sakate hai:pehla kadam:online inakam tex daakhil karne kii prakriya ko i-filing (e-filing) kehete hai

 go to in doosraa kadam:i-filing ke liye sabase pehle is website par apana acount bananaa hoga
